	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">

<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Uruguayan footballer</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">In this <a href="/wiki/Spanish_name" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish name">Spanish name</a>, the first or paternal&#32;<a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">surname</a> is <i> Cavani</i>&#32;and the second or maternal family name is <i> Gómez</i>.</div>

<p><b>Edinson Roberto Cavani Gómez</b> (<small>Spanish pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[eðinso kaani]</a></span>; born 14 February 1987) is a Uruguayan professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay national team</a>.
</p><p>Cavani began his career playing for <a href="/wiki/Danubio_F.C." title="Danubio F.C.">Danubio</a> in Montevideo, where he played for two years, before moving to Italian side <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> in 2007. He spent four seasons at the club, scoring 34 goals in 109 league appearances. In 2010, Cavani signed for <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, who signed him on an initial loan deal before buying him for a total fee of 17&#160;million. In the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_S.S.C._Napoli_season" title="201112 S.S.C. Napoli season">201112 season</a>, he won his first club honour, the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Coppa_Italia" title="201112 Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a>, in which he was top scorer with five goals. With Napoli, Cavani went on to score 33 goals each in his first two seasons, followed by 38 goals in his third season, where he also finished as <a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Serie A top scorer</a> with 29 league goals. 
</p><p>On 16 July 2013, Cavani was transferred to Paris Saint-Germain for a reported 64&#160;million, at the time the most expensive signing in French football history.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> With PSG, Cavani won six <a href="/wiki/List_of_French_football_champions" title="List of French football champions">Ligue 1 titles</a>, five <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupes de la Ligue</a> and four <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupes de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He won <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year" title="Ligue 1 Player of the Year">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Ligue_1" title="201617 Ligue 1">201617 season</a>, and was the league's <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ligue_1_top_scorers" title="List of Ligue 1 top scorers">top scorer</a> in the 201617 and <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Ligue_1" title="201718 Ligue 1">201718</a> seasons. He also ranks as the club's all-time top goalscorer.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In 2020, Cavani signed with Manchester United.
</p><p>Cavani scored on his <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> debut against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> on 6 February 2008, and has since then earned 117 caps and scored 51 international goals, only fewer than strike partner <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a> among Uruguayan internationals. He has participated in eight major international tournaments: the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2011 Copa América">2011 Copa América</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>. He scored once at the 2010 World Cup to help Uruguay to fourth place in the tournament, and in 2011 was part of the Uruguay squad that won a record 15th Copa América title. He finished as the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">CONMEBOL 2018 World Cup qualification</a> top scorer with 10 goals.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Palermo">Palermo</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">To this day. Batistuta wasn't a typical striker. A powerful footballer who was incredibly effective in front of goal. I always tried to copy him.</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Cavani on his idol growing up, <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Batistuta" title="Gabriel Batistuta">Gabriel Batistuta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>After his breakthrough at the 2007 South American Youth Championship, several big teams were reportedly interested in signing Cavani, including <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> and <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> On 29 January 2007, however, <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> chairman <a href="/wiki/Maurizio_Zamparini" title="Maurizio Zamparini">Maurizio Zamparini</a> announced the signing of the promising Uruguayan.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> The bid was officially confirmed on 31 January<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> for 4.475&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Cavani made his debut on 11 March 2007 in a home league match against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> coming on in the 55th minute with his team 10 down and scoring an impressive equaliser only 15 minutes later, a goal reminiscent of <a href="/wiki/Marco_van_Basten" title="Marco van Basten">Marco van Basten</a>'s strike in the <a href="/wiki/1988_UEFA_European_Football_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="1988 UEFA European Football Championship">1988 UEFA European Football Championship</a> final.<sup id="cite_ref-cbcsports_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cbcsports-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In his second season with the <i>Rosanero</i>, Cavani found himself fighting for a first team place with <a href="/wiki/Fabrizio_Miccoli" title="Fabrizio Miccoli">Fabrizio Miccoli</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amauri" title="Amauri">Amauri</a>.
</p><p>After Amauri's departure to Juventus in June 2008, Cavani cemented his place in the starting lineup, forming a striking partnership with Fabrizio Miccoli and scoring a total 14 goals in the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Serie_A" title="200809 Serie A">200809 season</a>, earning the nickname "<i>El Matador</i>" due to his composure in front of goal.<sup id="cite_ref-nickname_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nickname-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He retained his place for the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Serie_A" title="200910 Serie A">200910 season</a> under new boss <a href="/wiki/Walter_Zenga" title="Walter Zenga">Walter Zenga</a>, and also under successor <a href="/wiki/Delio_Rossi" title="Delio Rossi">Delio Rossi</a>, being instrumental in the team's successful run in <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> which took Palermo to European qualification and potential qualification to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> with two games remaining. In April 2010, he signed a new contract with Palermo valid to June 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Napoli">Napoli</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311:_Move_to_Europe"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201011:_Move_to_Europe">201011: Move to Europe</span></h4>
<p>In July 2010, Cavani signed for <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>. The transfer, however, was a loan of 5&#160;million plus an option/obligation to buy outright for 12&#160;million,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> which made the total fee 17&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> After debuting for Napoli as a substitute in the previous game, Cavani scored twice in his first start, as Napoli beat <a href="/wiki/IF_Elfsborg" title="IF Elfsborg">Elfsborg</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201011 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> 20 and qualified for the main tournament. He then started his Serie A tenure with Napoli in spectacular fashion, scoring a controversial goal against Fiorentina after just seven minutes, with replays showing the ball hardly crossing the line. Cavani also scored on his home debut against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Bari" class="mw-redirect" title="A.S. Bari">Bari</a> before adding a late winner against <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a>, meaning he had scored in his first four competitive matches with Napoli.
</p><p>On 26 September, Cavani came on as a late replacement with 30 minutes left in a game against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Cesena" title="A.C. Cesena">Cesena</a> which Napoli were losing 10. After assisting the equalizing goal, he went on to score two more, with the scoreline finishing at 41. That meant Cavani shared the lead as top scorer in the league alongside <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Internazionale</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Eto%27o" title="Samuel Eto&#39;o">Samuel Eto'o</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Cavani's partnership with fellow forwards <a href="/wiki/Ezequiel_Lavezzi" title="Ezequiel Lavezzi">Ezequiel Lavezzi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marek_Ham%C5%A1%C3%ADk" title="Marek Hamík">Marek Hamík</a> led the Italian sporting media to dub them "The Three Tenors" after the famous <a href="/wiki/The_Three_Tenors" title="The Three Tenors">singing group</a> of the same name. On 15 December, Cavani netted a 92nd-minute goal against <a href="/wiki/FC_Steaua_Bucure%C8%99ti" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Steaua Bucureti">Steaua Bucureti</a> to help his team to a 10 win and progress beyond the group stage of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>. In the first match, which was held on Romanian soil, he had scored an equalizing goal in the 97th minute. On 9 January 2011, Cavani scored a hat-trick during a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, the third goal coming by way of a diving header.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> On 30 January, Cavani scored another hat-trick, this time in a 40 win over Sampdoria.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Cavani continued his fine form scoring a brace against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, with Napoli winning 20.
</p><p>On 20 March, Cavani scored another brace against <a href="/wiki/Cagliari_Calcio" title="Cagliari Calcio">Cagliari</a> in a 21 win. This win kept them within three points of leaders Milan with eight games left. On 3 April, Cavani scored yet another hat-trick in a 43 comeback win over <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>, having been 20 and 32 down during the game. He also became the highest league goalscorer in a single season in Napoli's history, netting 25 goals in Serie A.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 8 May, in a 21 away loss against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Lecce" title="U.S. Lecce">Lecce</a>, he received a red card for having two booked offenses. He sarcastically applauded the referee after the decision and was handed a two-match ban for the action.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> As Napoli only had two more games of the season, it meant that his season was over and that he would not be able to regain his top position in the Serie A scoring charts, as <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Di_Natale" title="Antonio Di Natale">Antonio Di Natale</a> had surpassed him with 26 goals. Cavani signed a new five-year contract on 19 May, keeping him at Napoli until 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312:_Coppa_Italia_win"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201112:_Coppa_Italia_win">201112: Coppa Italia win</span></h4>
<p>On 14 September, Cavani scored the opener in Napoli's first game of their <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201112 UEFA Champions League">Champions League campaign</a>, a 11 away draw at <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, on 18 September, he scored a hat-trick against Milan in Napoli's 31 home win.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> On 22 November, Cavani scored both goals in the match winning brace 21 at home against Manchester City in the Champions League, leaving Napoli in pole position to follow <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> into the knockout stage.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> On 26 November, Cavani scored a 94th-minute equaliser against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a> after Napoli went a goal down in the 64th minute through on-loan Napoli striker <a href="/wiki/Germ%C3%A1n_Denis" title="Germán Denis">Germán Denis</a>. On 21 December, Cavani netted a brace in Napoli's 61 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>, helping the <i>Azzurri</i> finish 2011 strong and end the first half of the season in sixth place.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 February 2012, Cavani scored two goals against Fiorentina, helping Napoli go in fifth place ahead of Internazionale.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 21 February, Cavani scored the second goal against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in the Champions League round of 16 first leg in <a href="/wiki/Naples" title="Naples">Naples</a>. He also provided the assists for both of Ezequiel Lavezzi's goals that game. Napoli subsequently went on to win this game 31.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Following Napoli's exit from the Champions League at the hands of Chelsea, Cavani scored two goals against <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a> in the last ten minutes to earn a much-needed draw to keep Napoli in the hunt for the last Champions League qualifying spot. A few days later, he converted a fantastic counter-attack against <a href="/wiki/S.S._Robur_Siena" class="mw-redirect" title="S.S. Robur Siena">Siena</a> to book Napoli a place in the <a href="/wiki/2012_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2012 Coppa Italia Final">Coppa Italia final</a>. On 21 April, he celebrated his 200th career league appearance by scoring in a 20 win against <a href="/wiki/Novara_Calcio" title="Novara Calcio">Novara</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Cavani finished the league season with 23 goals,<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> tied for third on the goal scoring charts with Udinese striker Antonio Di Natale.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 20 May, Cavani scored a penalty against Juventus in the 2012 Coppa Italia final at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a>, Rome, which Napoli won 20.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Cavani finished the tournament as the top goalscorer, with five goals.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313:_Serie_A_top_scorer"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201213:_Serie_A_top_scorer">201213: Serie A top scorer</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Edinson_Cavani_(vs._AIK_in_2012,_cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Edinson_Cavani_%28vs._AIK_in_2012%2C_cropped%29.jpg/220px-Edinson_Cavani_%28vs._AIK_in_2012%2C_cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="149" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/be/Edinson_Cavani_%28vs._AIK_in_2012%2C_cropped%29.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="329" data-file-height="223" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Edinson_Cavani_(vs._AIK_in_2012,_cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani playing against <a href="/wiki/AIK_Fotboll" title="AIK Fotboll">AIK</a> in the Europa League</div></div></div>
<p>Cavani's first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Serie_A" title="201213 Serie A">Serie A</a> season came on 26 August, netting the final goal of Napoli's 30 defeat of former club Palermo.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> A month later, on 26 September, Cavani scored a mesmerizing hat-trick against Lazio to maintain Napoli's undefeated start to the Serie A season in a 30 win.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 8 November, Cavani scored all four goals, including a half-volley from outside the box and a tremendous free kick, as Napoli came back from 21 down to defeat <a href="/wiki/FC_Dnipro_Dnipropetrovsk" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Dnipro Dnipropetrovsk">Dnipro Dnipropetrovsk</a> 42 in the group stage of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201213 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Cavani scored a late penalty in the 94th minute to secure a 21 victory over Swedish side <a href="/wiki/AIK_Fotboll" title="AIK Fotboll">AIK</a> on 22 November, sending Napoli through to the next round of the Europa League.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Cavani was the last player ever to score on the <a href="/wiki/R%C3%A5sunda_Stadium" title="Råsunda Stadium">Råsunda Stadium</a> which was the stadium that hosted the <a href="/wiki/1958_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1958 FIFA World Cup">1958 FIFA World Cup</a> final.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On 6 January 2013, Cavani netted a perfect hat-trick as Napoli thumped Roma 41, gaining ground in the race for the league title as champions Juventus fell to a shock win.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Cavani finished the season as leading Serie A goalscorer, with 29 goals, six ahead of Udinese striker Antonio Di Natale in second.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Towards the end of the season, reports emerged that Cavani would leave Napoli, with Chelsea, Manchester City, <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> all believed to be interested.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 27 May 2013, however, he told that he was not thinking of moving, saying, "Real Madrid, Chelsea and [Manchester] City are interested in me? I just think about Napoli." Nonetheless, he continued, "If an important offer were to come in, I will talk with president [Aurelio] De Laurentiis." He then paid tribute to his time in Italy, saying, "I'm fine in Italy, I have grown as a man there and as a player with the Serie A experience."<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Cavani was asked about the interest Chelsea and Manchester City took in him, saying, "I don't know if they made an offer for me, I just know that to be coached by someone like [Man City manager] <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Pellegrini" title="Manuel Pellegrini">Manuel Pellegrini</a> or [Chelsea manager] <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> would always be a pleasure."<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 23 June, Napoli club president <a href="/wiki/Aurelio_De_Laurentiis" title="Aurelio De Laurentiis">Aurelio De Laurentiis</a> revealed that Cavani's reported £53&#160;million "buyout clause expires" on 10 August 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:132px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Edinson_Cavani,_PSG.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG/130px-Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG" decoding="async" width="130" height="246" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG/195px-Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG/260px-Edinson_Cavani%2C_PSG.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1690" data-file-height="3196" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Edinson_Cavani,_PSG.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani with PSG in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 16 July 2013, Cavani joined French champions Paris Saint-Germain on a five-year contract,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> for a fee believed to be around 64&#160;million,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> making it the sixth <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">largest transfer in history</a>. The reported sum made Cavani the record signing in French football, breaking <a href="/wiki/Radamel_Falcao" title="Radamel Falcao">Radamel Falcao</a>'s 60&#160;million move to <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> earlier in the summer, and saw him link up with former Napoli teammate Ezequiel Lavezzi in Paris.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314:_Debut_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314:_Debut_season">201314: Debut season</span></h4>
<p>Cavani debuted for PSG on 9 August, coming on as 72nd-minute substitute for Lavezzi in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He started the following game on 18 August and scored his first goal for the club, a late equaliser against <a href="/wiki/AC_Ajaccio" title="AC Ajaccio">Ajaccio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani scored his first Champions League goal for the club in their European season opener against <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a> on 17 September.<sup id="cite_ref-uefa_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uefa-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> He ended the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201314 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> with four goals from five matches as PSG qualified with a 100% win record.<sup id="cite_ref-uefa_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-uefa-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 January 2014, Cavani scored his 20th goal of the season in PSG's 21 <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Coupe_de_France" title="201314 Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a> defeat at home to Montpellier.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March, after missing a month of the season with a thigh injury, Cavani scored on his return to the team in a 20 win over <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Classique" title="Le Classique">Le Classique</a></i> rivals <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 April, he scored both goals for PSG as they beat <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a> 21 in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2014 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2014 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He finished his first season with 25 goals in 43 games across all competitions, including 16 in 30 league games.
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9316:_Back-to-back_domestic_quadruples"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201416:_Back-to-back_domestic_quadruples">201416: Back-to-back domestic quadruples</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:PSG-Shakhter15_(8).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg/170px-PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="206" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg/255px-PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg/339px-PSG-Shakhter15_%288%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="483" data-file-height="586" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:PSG-Shakhter15_(8).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani playing for PSG in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in October 2015</div></div></div>
<p>Cavani scored a penalty to secure a 31 win at <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a> on 17 October 2014, and <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">celebrated</a> by shooting an imaginary gun. Referee Nicolas Rainville booked him for this, and sent him off for dissent after Cavani complained about it. PSG club president <a href="/wiki/Nasser_Al-Khelaifi" title="Nasser Al-Khelaifi">Nasser Al-Khelaifi</a> said to <a href="/wiki/Canal%2B" title="Canal+">Canal+</a>, "Why did he get the yellow card before? He always celebrates the same way."<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 5 November 2014, it took Cavani 56 seconds to score the only goal of the game against Cypriot club <a href="/wiki/APOEL_FC" title="APOEL FC">APOEL</a>, a result which put PSG into the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201415 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_stage" class="mw-redirect" title="201415 UEFA Champions League knockout stage">knock-out stage</a> with two games to spare.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2015, Cavani and Ezequiel Lavezzi were fined and suspended for two matches by PSG manager <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Blanc" title="Laurent Blanc">Laurent Blanc</a> for missing a mid-season training camp in Morocco and the first training session after the winter break.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 11 April, he scored two goals as a second-half substitute for Lavezzi as PSG defeated <a href="/wiki/SC_Bastia" title="SC Bastia">Bastia</a> 40 to win the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2015 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2015 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On 8 May, he scored a hat-trick in a 60 defeat of <a href="/wiki/En_Avant_de_Guingamp" class="mw-redirect" title="En Avant de Guingamp">Guingamp</a>, which gave PSG a six-point lead in <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Ligue_1" title="201415 Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> with two matches remaining.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> With the title retained, PSG sealed a domestic treble on 30 May when Cavani headed the only goal of the game  his 31st in all competitions that season  to defeat <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a> in the Coupe de France final.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani and PSG kicked off the season against Lyon for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2015 Trophée des Champions">2015 Trophée des Champions</a> on 1 August, with him scoring the second goal of a 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> On 21 May 2016, Cavani scored the decisive third goal of PSG's 42 <a href="/wiki/2016_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2016 Coupe de France Final">2016 Coupe de France Final</a> win over Marseille to record a second consecutive <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Ligue_1" title="201516 Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Coupe_de_France" title="201516 Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="201516 Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> domestic treble for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9318:_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year.2C_back-to-back_Golden_Boots"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201618:_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year,_back-to-back_Golden_Boots">201618: Ligue 1 Player of the Year, back-to-back Golden Boots</span></h4>
<p>On 13 September 2016, in the opening <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201617 UEFA Champions League group stage">201617 Champions League</a> Group A match against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> at the Parc des Princes, Cavani scored after just 44 seconds had elapsed in the first half by heading in <a href="/wiki/Serge_Aurier" title="Serge Aurier">Serge Aurier</a>'s cross from the right for PSG's fastest-ever Champions League goal. The match ended in a 11 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 16 September, Cavani scored four times (his first ever four-goal haul with PSG) in the first half as PSG trounced <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> 60 away in a <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Ligue_1" title="201617 Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> match to end PSG's streak of three competitive matches without victory, two of them in Ligue 1.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 30 November, he scored a penalty in a 20 home win against <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a> to take his Ligue 1 tally to 14 goals in 14 matches,<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> which also saw him become only the fourth player in PSG history to score 100 competitive goals for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani scored one goal in each leg of PSG's 65 aggregate loss to <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">FC Barcelona</a> in their <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="201617 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">UEFA Champions League round of 16</a> tie, taking him to eight goals from eight matches in the season's competition. On 1 April 2017, he scored two-second-half goals in PSG's 41 win over <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Coupe_de_la_Ligue#Final" title="201617 Coupe de la Ligue">2017 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> On 15 May 2017, he was named <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year" title="Ligue 1 Player of the Year">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a> for scoring 35 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_(16172587073).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg/220px-2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg/330px-2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg/440px-2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_%2816172587073%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="3456" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_CHE_PSG_DSC02652_(16172587073).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani (number 9, standing next to <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a>, number 10, in March 2015) surpassed his former PSG teammate to become the club's all-time record goalscorer in 2018</div></div></div>
<p>Prior to the 201718 season, Cavani was joined at the club by Brazilian forward <a href="/wiki/Neymar" title="Neymar">Neymar</a>, who moved to PSG in a transaction worth 222&#160;million making him <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">the world's most expensive player</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> and 18-year-old French prodigy <a href="/wiki/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9" title="Kylian Mbappé">Kylian Mbappé</a>, a loan signing with the club having an option to sign him for 180&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Cavani, Neymar and Mbappé immediately formed a formidable attacking trio, with Cavani scoring in each of PSG's opening three games of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201718 UEFA Champions League group stage">201718 UEFA Champions League group stage</a>, twice in the team's 50 win at <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a>, once in the 30 win at home to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>, and once in the 40 win at <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 October, Cavani scored a curling free kick off the crossbar to earn PSG a 22 draw in <a href="/wiki/Le_Classique" title="Le Classique">Le Classique</a> away to <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> The following month, he scored twice in the return leg against Celtic in a 71 win. The result saw PSG break the record for the most goals scored by a club in the group stages of the Champions League, with 24.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 4 November, Cavani's goals in a 50 win at <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a> made him only the third player to score 100 times in two of Europe's five best leagues, after Ibrahimovi and <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani became PSG's all-time top scorer on 27 January 2018 with a goal in a 40 home win over <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>. He surpassed <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a>'s record with his 157th goal in his 229th match.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> On 8 May 2018, he scored as PSG won 20 against <a href="/wiki/Les_Herbiers_VF" title="Les Herbiers VF">Les Herbiers VF</a> to clinch the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Coupe_de_France" title="201718 Coupe de France">201718 Coupe de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9320:_Final_seasons_in_Paris"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201820:_Final_seasons_in_Paris">201820: Final seasons in Paris</span></h4>
<p>On 25 August 2018, Cavani played his first game of the season after missing PSG's first three games following his injury at the 2018 World Cup. The front three of Cavani, Neymar and Mbappé all scored in a 31 league win over <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a> at home, with Cavani scoring the opener from Neymar's assist.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> On 11 November 2018, Cavani scored a hat-trick in a 40 win over <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 18 December, Cavani scored in PSG's 21 win over <a href="/wiki/US_Orl%C3%A9ans" title="US Orléans">Orléans</a> in the Coupe de La Ligue; this was his 15th goal all-time in the competition, tying <a href="/wiki/Pauleta" title="Pauleta">Pauleta</a>'s record for most goals in the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In April 2020, PSG were assigned the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Ligue_1" title="201920 Ligue 1">201920 Ligue 1</a> title after the season was ended prematurely due to the outbreak of the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>; at the time of the League's suspension, PSG were in first place, with a twelvepoint lead over second-placed Marseille.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> On 13 June, PSG's sporting director <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Ara%C3%BAjo" title="Leonardo Araújo">Leonardo</a> revealed that Cavani would be leaving the club at the end of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201920 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> campaign in August, alongside his teammate <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Silva" title="Thiago Silva">Thiago Silva</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_United">Manchester United</span></h3>
<p>On 5 October 2020, Cavani joined Premier League club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> on a one-year deal with an option to extend for a further year.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> He was given the prestigious number 7 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> On 24 October 2020, he made his Premier League debut from the bench in a 00 draw against Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> On 7 November, Cavani scored his first goal in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> in a 31 away win against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 29 November, Cavani scored twice, including the winning goal in added time, in a 32 comeback win against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 February 2021, he scored the fourth goal in United's Premier League record-equalling <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C._9%E2%80%930_Southampton_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C. 90 Southampton F.C.">90</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Schaars_Cavani.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Schaars_Cavani.jpg/170px-Schaars_Cavani.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="222" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Schaars_Cavani.jpg/255px-Schaars_Cavani.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Schaars_Cavani.jpg/340px-Schaars_Cavani.jpg 2x" data-file-width="826" data-file-height="1079" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Schaars_Cavani.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani (right) with <a href="/wiki/Stijn_Schaars" title="Stijn Schaars">Stijn Schaars</a> of the Netherlands in June 2011</div></div></div>
<p>In January 2007, Cavani was selected to join the <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_under-20_football_team" title="Uruguay national under-20 football team">Uruguay national under-20 team</a> to play in the <a href="/wiki/2007_South_American_Youth_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2007 South American Youth Championship">2007 South American Youth Championship</a> in Paraguay. Cavani finished the tournament as top scorer with seven goals in nine games, helping Uruguay to finish in third place, thereby earning them a place in the <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2007 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_América">2010 World Cup and 2011 Copa América</span></h4>
<p>On 6 February 2008, Cavani made his first senior appearance for the <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguayan senior team</a>, scoring in a 22 draw with <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a>. He scored from his own area on the counterattack from a corner.
</p><p>On 22 June 2010, in the final match of the group stage of the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>, Cavani set-up a goal for <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a> in a 10 win over <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFA_Uru-Mex_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFA_Uru-Mex-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hassan_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hassan-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Uruguay won <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_Group_A" title="2010 FIFA World Cup Group A">Group A</a> and advanced to the <a href="/wiki/Single-elimination_tournament" title="Single-elimination tournament">knockout stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFA_Uru-Mex_92-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFA_Uru-Mex-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hassan_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hassan-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> On 10 July 2010, he scored against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in the third place match to make the score 11; Germany went on to win 32.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 8 October 2010, he scored his first international <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Indonesia_national_football_team" title="Indonesia national football team">Indonesia</a>, a 71 win in <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a> in which Luis Suárez also scored a hat-trick.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani was included in the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_squads#Uruguay" title="2011 Copa América squads">Uruguayan squad</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2011 Copa América">2011 Copa América</a> in Argentina. He started the first two group games, but a knee injury in the second game against <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> ruled him out until the final. In <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Final" title="2011 Copa América Final">the final</a>, he replaced <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Pereira" title="Álvaro Pereira">Álvaro Pereira</a> after 63 minutes, and was involved in his team's final goal as Uruguay won a record 15th title by beating <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a> 30.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012_Olympics.2C_2013_Confederations_Cup.2C_and_2014_World_Cup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012_Olympics,_2013_Confederations_Cup,_and_2014_World_Cup">2012 Olympics, 2013 Confederations Cup, and 2014 World Cup</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg/220px-1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="153" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg/330px-1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg/440px-1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5283" data-file-height="3675" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1_edinson_cavani_2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani waiting to take a free-kick in the Round of 16 game against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Round_of_16" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>Cavani was one of the three over-age players selected by Uruguay for the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>, Cavani equalised in the semi-final against the hosts and eventual champions <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>, who eventually won 21.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> In the match for third place, he equalised twice against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, his second goal coming from a free kick, taking the game to penalties. Although Cavani scored his spot kick, Uruguay lost; he was named man of the match for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 November 2013, Cavani scored the last goal in Uruguay's 50 away win over <a href="/wiki/Jordan_national_football_team" title="Jordan national football team">Jordan</a> in a play-off for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> In their first group game of the finals, against <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica_national_football_team" title="Costa Rica national football team">Costa Rica</a> in <a href="/wiki/Fortaleza" title="Fortaleza">Fortaleza</a>, Cavani opened the scoring with a penalty after <a href="/wiki/Diego_Lugano" title="Diego Lugano">Diego Lugano</a> had been pulled down. Uruguay, however, eventually lost 31.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Uruguay were eliminated by Colombia, following a 20 defeat in the round of 16 on 28 June 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-World_Cup">Post-World Cup</span></h4>
<p>With Suárez suspended for the entire tournament, Cavani was an undisputed starter for Uruguay at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a> in Chile. In the quarter-finals against the hosts at the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Nacional_Julio_Mart%C3%ADnez_Pr%C3%A1danos" title="Estadio Nacional Julio Martínez Prádanos">Estadio Nacional</a>, Cavani was sent off for two bookings: the first for a foul on <a href="/wiki/Arturo_Vidal" title="Arturo Vidal">Arturo Vidal</a>, the second for flicking at <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Jara" title="Gonzalo Jara">Gonzalo Jara</a>'s face after Jara had poked him in the buttocks. The incident received almost immediate and prominent international coverage from newspapers and the internet, mostly in defense of Cavani. Massive coverage included articles, columns, blogs, memes and cartoons. Press in Australia drew comparisons to what the press referred to as "<a href="/wiki/John_Hopoate" title="John Hopoate">Hopoate</a>", comparing it to a similar infamous onfield anus-poking incident from rugby.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Other massive international coverage of the incident came from China,<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> the United Kingdom,<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> France,<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> and the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> Internet coverage included Goal.com,<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Business Insider,<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> ESPNFC,<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Bleacher Report<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_World_Game" title="The World Game">The World Game</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Huffington_Post" class="mw-redirect" title="The Huffington Post">The Huffington Post</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> and Dirty Tackle.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Teammate <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Fucile" title="Jorge Fucile">Jorge Fucile</a> was later also dismissed, and holders Uruguay were eliminated with a 10 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> Cavani also took part in the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a> the following year, but he once again went scoreless in the competition, as Uruguay were eliminated in the first round.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:URU-POR_(13).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg/200px-URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="152" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg/300px-URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg/400px-URU-POR_%2813%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1584" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:URU-POR_(13).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani being helped off the field by <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> after Uruguay's win over Portugal at the 2018 World Cup</div></div></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span></h4>
<p>Cavani finished as the top scorer in the <a href="/wiki/CONMEBOL" title="CONMEBOL">CONMEBOL</a> <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a>, with 10 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> In March 2018, Cavani was part of the Uruguay squad that won the <a href="/wiki/China_Cup" title="China Cup">China Cup</a>. He scored in the 20 semi-final win over the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_football_team" title="Czech Republic national football team">Czech Republic</a>, and in the final he scored the only goal against <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_football_team" title="Wales national football team">Wales</a>, his <a href="/wiki/List_of_men%27s_footballers_with_100_or_more_international_caps" title="List of men&#39;s footballers with 100 or more international caps">100th cap</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his nation's final group game of the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> on 25 June, Cavani scored Uruguay's final goal in a 30 win over hosts <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> Cavani then went on to score both of Uruguay's goals against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> in a 21 victory in the Round of 16 on 30 June,<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> though he was withdrawn in the second-half with an apparent hamstring injury.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> Because of his injury, he was ruled out of Uruguay's 20 defeat to <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in the quarter-finals on 6 July.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019_Copa_América">2019 Copa América</span></h4>
<p>In March 2019, manager <a href="/wiki/%C3%93scar_Tab%C3%A1rez" title="Óscar Tabárez">Óscar Tabárez</a> included Cavani in the final 23-man Uruguay squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a> in Brazil.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> On 16 June, Cavani scored "an acrobatic <a href="/wiki/Bicycle_kick" title="Bicycle kick">bicycle-kick</a>" in a 40 win over <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_football_team" title="Ecuador national football team">Ecuador</a> in the team's opening group match of the tournament;<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> this was his first goal ever in the Copa América.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> In the quarter-finals against <a href="/wiki/Peru_national_football_team" title="Peru national football team">Peru</a> on 29 June, he had a goal disallowed by VAR for offside in regulation time; following a 00 draw, the match went to a penalty shoot-out. Although Cavani was able to convert his spot-kick, Peru won the shoot-out 54, which saw Uruguay eliminated from the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_(Cavani).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg/250px-Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg/375px-Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg/500px-Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_%28Cavani%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="3000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hungary_-_Uruguay_0-1_(Cavani).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cavani in the air (<a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a>  Uruguay 01)</div></div></div>
<p>A quick, strong, opportunistic and prolific <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> with good technique, and a tall, slender frame, Cavani has been described as a "modern striker."<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> Possessing an excellent first touch, intelligent movement off the ball, and clinical finishing, he is a well-rounded striker,<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> who is known for his ability to score impressive goals, both with his head and with his feet, and for his tireless work-rate and energy across the pitch, as well as his willingness to track back and help his team defensively; moreover, he is an athletic player, who is also strong in the air, and who has a penchant for scoring from acrobatic goals. He is also an accurate <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">set-piece</a> taker,<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_Should_Be_Satisfied_137-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_Should_Be_Satisfied-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_and_Luis_Suarez_Would_Thrive_Leading_Liverpool_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_and_Luis_Suarez_Would_Thrive_Leading_Liverpool-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> and is generally a competent <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> taker, even though his record from the spot has been inconsistent at times throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>In addition to his goalscoring, he is also known for his ability to create space for his teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_defends_display_142-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_defends_display-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> However, despite being a prolific player, and having a reputation as one of the best strikers of his generation,<sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit_135-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> he has been accused at times in the media of missing an excessive number of chances, and has also been criticised on occasion for his performances in important matches.<sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit_135-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_Reportedly_Eyeing_PSG_Exit-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Although he primarily plays either as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre forward</a> or as a main striker, he is capable of playing in several offensive positions, and has also been deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">supporting striker</a> or as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">winger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_and_Luis_Suarez_Would_Thrive_Leading_Liverpool_138-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_and_Luis_Suarez_Would_Thrive_Leading_Liverpool-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Cavani_defends_display_142-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cavani_defends_display-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> Writing for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> in 2018, <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Valdano" title="Jorge Valdano">Jorge Valdano</a> remarked upon "the generous endeavour of Cavani, a striker who covers the entire pitch".<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> Due to his composure in front of goal, Cavani was given the nickname "<i><a href="/wiki/Bullfighter" title="Bullfighter">El Matador</a></i>" during his time in Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-nickname_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nickname-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<p>Cavani was born in <a href="/wiki/Salto,_Uruguay" title="Salto, Uruguay">Salto, Uruguay</a> on 14 February, 1987 to Luis Cavani and Berta Gómez.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> His elder brothers, striker <a href="/wiki/Walter_Guglielmone" title="Walter Guglielmone">Walter Guglielmone</a><sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> and Christian Cavani, are also professional footballers.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> Cavani holds an <a href="/wiki/Italian_passport" title="Italian passport">Italian passport</a> as a result of playing in Italy and his <a href="/wiki/Italian_Uruguayans" title="Italian Uruguayans">Italian</a> heritage; Cavani's grandparents were originally from <a href="/wiki/Maranello" title="Maranello">Maranello</a>. In 1929, they migrated to Argentina and later to <a href="/wiki/Montevideo" title="Montevideo">Montevideo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Cavani was married to Maria Soledad Cabris Yarrús, with whom he has two sons, Bautista (born 22 March 2011) and Lucas (born 8 March 2013).<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> In 2013, Cavani announced that he and his wife were to get a divorce, following a split between the two the year before.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> Then he had a daughter, India (born 17 May 2019), with his girlfriend Jocelyn Burgardt.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is a devout <a href="/wiki/Evangelicalism" title="Evangelicalism">Evangelical</a> Christian.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> As a child, Cavani idolised Argentine striker <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Batistuta" title="Gabriel Batistuta">Gabriel Batistuta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> Cavani also enjoys <a href="/wiki/Ballet" title="Ballet">ballet</a> dancing.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span></h2>
